Marvel Masterworks Original Design (1987-2026)

In Marvel Previews (I) #23 a list of all Marvel Masterworks volumes published so far was given, which are expand with the new volumes since then. The volumes 1 to 27 were reprinted in the according 2nd series with the same number, but sometimes with a different contents. For all volumes since 2002 there are variant covers that match the original cover design.
